# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Grafana Legacy Alerting to Unified Alerting Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement both the legacy alerting engine and the unified alerting (ngalert) engine: the legacy alert rule storage, the unified alert rule storage, and the migration script that converts legacy rules to unified format.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` (grafana/grafana)
- `sg-evals/grafana-loki` (grafana/loki)
- `sg-evals/grafana-mimir` (grafana/mimir)

```json
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Summary of Findings

I've identified **25 core files** across the grafana/grafana repository implementing these systems:

### **Legacy Alerting Engine**
- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go` - Defines legacy alert tables (alert, alert_notification, alert_rule_tag)

### **Unified Alerting (ngalert) Storage**
- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go` - Main unified alert rule storage (DBstore)
- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go` - All unified alerting table definitions
- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alertmanager.go` - Alertmanager-specific storage
- `pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go` - Core alert rule models

### **Legacy Storage Wrappers (Backward Compatibility)**
- Legacy notifier storage: config, compat, imported, routes, receivers, inhibition_rules
- Registry apps layers: alert rule, recording rule, receiver, and routing tree legacy storage

### **Migration & Conversion Scripts**
- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/ualert.go` - Main migration engine (upgradeNgAlerting)
- `pkg/services/ngalert/api/api_convert_prometheus.go` - ConvertPrometheusSrv for Prometheus rule conversion
- `pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/alert_rules.go` - AlertRuleService provisioning API
- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/compat.go` - Compatibility layer for format conversion

The answer.json file at `/workspace/answer.json` contains the complete structured documentation with all files, key symbols, the migration chain, and detailed narrative explanation.

alertmanager configurations for backward compatibility\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/compat.go**: Contains conversion functions like InhibitRuleToInhibitionRule for converting legacy format to unified format\\n\\n- **pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/imported.go**: Handles imported legacy configurations (especially from Prometheus/external sources) with the Handles organization assignment for configurations\\n4. Includes FixEarlyMigration for handling configurations created before version 8.2 with org_id=0\\n\\n**pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go**: Defines all database table migrations for configurations\\n3. **NewConvertPrometheusSrv**: Initializes the conversion service with rule store, datasource cache, and alert rule service\\n\\nThis service enables importing rules from Mimir and other Prometheus-compatible systems while preserving the original rule definitions for round-trip compatibility.\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/api/prometheus_conversion.go**: Handler wrapper for the conversion API endpoints\\n\\n#### Compatibility Layer\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/store/compat.go**: Provides compatibility functions for converting between legacy and new formats:\\n- convertAlertRuleToModel: Converts alertRule database objects to ngalert models.AlertRule\\n- AlertRuleConvertOptions: Controls which fields to parse during conversion\\n\\n#### Provisioning API\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/alert_rules.go**: Implements AlertRuleService for rule provisioning:\\n- Manages rule CRUD operations\\n- Handles rule group operations\\n- Manages provenance (who created/modified rules)\\n- Enforces access control\\n- Validates rule groups and quotas\\n- Integrates with folder service for namespace management\\n\\n**pkg/services/ngalert/api/api_provisioning.go**: Provisioning API implementation using AlertRuleService\\n\\n### Migration Flow\\n\\nThe migration path from legacy to unified alerting:\\n\\n1. **Legacy System** (dashboard alerts in alert table)\\n   \u2193\\n2. **Migration Code** (upgradeNgAlerting migration)\\n   \u2193\\n3. **Unified Storage** (alert_rule table and maintain backward compatibility by wrapping the unified storage while converting between legacy and new formats on-the-fly, allowing existing code and external tools (like mimirtool) to continue
